Ver. 1.56 - 7/31/2022 - "Baby Dragon Update"
======================
Additions:
+Added prefix/suffix naming for all cit renames: 
   ~Including the item rename's name in parenthesis anywhere in the anvil name will now make the texture show
   ~This means you can name your items while still using a custom anvil item texture
   ~An example of this being used could be: "Any Name (Hawkbrand)"
   ~The texture will show as the Hawkbrand anvil sword rename while still allowing a separate name
